9th-32nd Decklists
==================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 22, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/halliesanto_icon.jpg)
By Hallie Santo











Grand Prix Los Angeles showcased the breadth of Modern, and these decklists, piloted by our 9th through 32nd place finishers, provide a great snapshot of this diverse format. Whether you're interested in playing Grixis Control, Grishoalbrand, and Goblin Guides, you should find plenty of inspiration for your next Modern deck below.







#### Francis Cellona's Jeskai Harbinger - GP Los Angeles, 9th Place


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
